EU_council_category = {

	EU_council_update = {

		available = {
			#has_idea = EU_member
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea = EU_member
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = "Update EU Council voting prediction"
			hidden_effect = {
				EU_update_AI_specific_voting_modifiers = yes
				EU_update_voting_prediction_vars = yes
			}
		}

	}

#############################################
### EU Voting Rights Suspension Decisions ###
#############################################

### suspend EU voting rights ###


EU_council_determine_serious_breach_of_EU_values = {
	allowed = {
		is_EU_potential = yes
	}
	target_root_trigger = {
		has_idea = EU_member
	}
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
			}
		}
	}
	target_array = global.EU_potential
	cost = 100
	available = {
		FROM = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "Level of breach of EU values > 3."
				check_variable = { THIS.breach_of_EU_value > 3 }
			}
		}
		has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] must be top 3 influencer in all other (voting) member states than [FROM.GetNameWithFlag]."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					is_top3_influencer = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[FROM.GetNameWithFlag] must not be top 3 influencer in any other (voting) member states."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					NOT = { FROM_is_top3_influencer = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	visible = {
		#has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		FROM = {
			check_variable = { THIS.breach_of_EU_value > 3 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values }
		}
	}
	complete_effect = {
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic = 0.15 }
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic_target = THIS }
			eurosceptic_change = yes
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1

	}
}


EU_council_revoke_determination_of_serious_breach_of_EU_values = {
	allowed = {
		is_EU_potential = yes
	}
	target_root_trigger = {
		has_idea = EU_member
	}
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
		}
	}
	target_array = global.EU_potential
	cost = 100
	available = {
		FROM = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "Level of breach of EU values < 4."
				check_variable = { THIS.breach_of_EU_value < 4 }
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
		}
		has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] must be top 3 influencer in all other (voting) member states than [FROM.GetNameWithFlag]."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					is_top3_influencer = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	visible = {
		#has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		FROM = {
			has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
		}
	}
	complete_effect = {
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic = -0.15 }
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic_target = THIS }
			eurosceptic_change = yes
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1

	}
}

EU_council_suspend_voting_rights = {
	allowed = {
		is_EU_potential = yes
	}
	target_root_trigger = {
		has_idea = EU_member
	}
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
		}
	}
	target_array = global.EU_potential
	cost = 100
	available = {
		FROM = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "Level of breach of EU values > 4."
				check_variable = { THIS.breach_of_EU_value > 4 }
			}
		}
		has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] must be top 3 influencer in all other (voting) member states than [FROM.GetNameWithFlag]."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					is_top3_influencer = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[FROM.GetNameWithFlag] must not be top 3 influencer in any other (voting) member states."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					NOT = { FROM_is_top3_influencer = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	visible = {
		#has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		FROM = {
			has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
	}
	complete_effect = {
		FROM = {
			add_ideas = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic = 0.30 }
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic_target = THIS }
			eurosceptic_change = yes
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1

	}
}

EU_council_revoke_voting_rights_suspension = {
	allowed = {
		is_EU_potential = yes
	}
	target_root_trigger = {
		has_idea = EU_member
	}
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
	}
	target_array = global.EU_potential
	cost = 100
	available = {
		FROM = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "Level of breach of EU values < 5."
				check_variable = { THIS.breach_of_EU_value < 5 }
			}
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] must be top 3 influencer in all other (voting) member states than [FROM.GetNameWithFlag]."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					is_top3_influencer = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	visible = {
		#has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		FROM = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
	}
	complete_effect = {
		FROM = {
			remove_ideas = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic = -0.30 }
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic_target = THIS }
			eurosceptic_change = yes
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1

	}
}

EU_council_suspend_subsidies = {
	allowed = {
		is_EU_potential = yes
	}
	target_root_trigger = {
		has_idea = EU_member
	}
	target_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_subsidies_suspended
			}
		}
	}
	target_array = global.EU_potential
	cost = 100
	available = {
		FROM = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "Level of breach of EU values > 3."
				check_variable = { THIS.breach_of_EU_value > 3 }
			}
		}
		has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] must be top 3 influencer in all other (voting) member states than [FROM.GetNameWithFlag]."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					is_top3_influencer = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = "[FROM.GetNameWithFlag] must not be top 3 influencer in any other (voting) member states."
			all_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
						has_idea = EU_member
						NOT = {
							has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
						}
					}
					NOT = { FROM_is_top3_influencer = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	visible = {
		#has_idea = EU_member
		NOT = {
			has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
		}
		FROM = {
			has_country_flag = serious_breach_of_EU_values
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_subsidies_suspended }
		}
	}
	complete_effect = {
		FROM = {
			add_ideas = EUU_subsidies_suspended
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic = 0.20 }
			set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic_target = THIS }
			eurosceptic_change = yes
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1

	}
}

			country_event = {

			}
		}
	}
}

EU_AI_will_not_retry = {

	available = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = EU_no_retry }
		has_idea = EU_member
	}

	visible = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = EU_no_retry }
		has_idea = EU_member
	}

	complete_effect = {
		set_global_flag = EU_no_retry
	}
}

EU_AI_will_retry = {

	available = {
		has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
		has_idea = EU_member
	}

	visible = {
		has_global_flag = not_visible #EU_no_retry
		has_idea = EU_member
	}

	complete_effect = {
		clr_global_flag = EU_no_retry
	}
}


##################################
### 1.1.8 New Voting Decisions ###
##################################

	### EU Policies ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU001 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU001_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus EU Policies"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU001
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU001_voted
							focus_EU001_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU001
			NOT = {
				focus_EU001_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU001 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU001_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU001_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1001
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU001_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### EU Policies ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU001_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU001_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus EU Policies"
					AND = {

							focus_EU001_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {

			NOT = {
				focus_EU001_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU001 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU001_retry }

			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#

			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo

				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1001
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU001_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### EU Policies # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU001_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU001_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU001_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU001_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU001
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU001
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### EU Policies # Result Mission QMV ###

	### EU Policies retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU001_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU001_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU001 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU001_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU001
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU001_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU001
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU001
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU001_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Member State Policies ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU002 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU002_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Member State Policies"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU002
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU002_voted
							focus_EU002_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU002
			NOT = {
				focus_EU002_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU002 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU002_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU002_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU002_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1002
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU002_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Charter of Fundamental Rights of the European Union ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU101_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU101_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Charter of Fundamental Rights of the European Union"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU101_QMV_voted
							focus_EU101_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU101_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU101 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU101_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU101_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU101_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1101
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU101_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Charter of Fundamental Rights of the European Union # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU101_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU101_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU101_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU101_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU101
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU101
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### Charter of Fundamental Rights of the European Union retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU101_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU101_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU101 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU101_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU101
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU101_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU101_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU101_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU101
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU101_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU101
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU101_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU103_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU103
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU103_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Treaty of Lisbon ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU104 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU104_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Treaty of Lisbon"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU104
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU104_voted
							focus_EU104_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU104
			NOT = {
				focus_EU104_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU104 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU104_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			NOT = {
					focus_EU103_accepted = yes
			}
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU104_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU104_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1104
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU104_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

		}

	### Treaty of Lisbon # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU104_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU104_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU104_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU104_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU104
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU104
					}
				}
		}
	}

				clr_country_flag = focus_EU104_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU104_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU104
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU104_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU104
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU104_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

			}

			has_global_flag = focus_EU200_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU200_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU200_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU200
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU200
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### EU Fiscal Policies # Result Mission QMV ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU200_QMV_result = {

	### EU Fiscal Policies retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU200_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU200_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU200 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU200_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU200
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU200_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU200_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU200_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU200
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU200_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU200
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU200_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### ECB Intervention ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU201 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU201_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus ECB Intervention"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU201
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU201_voted
							focus_EU201_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU201
			NOT = {
				focus_EU201_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU201 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU201_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU201_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU201_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1201
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU201_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### ECB Intervention ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU201_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU201_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus ECB Intervention"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU201_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU201_QMV_voted
							focus_EU201_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU201_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU201_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU201 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU201_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU201_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU201_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1201
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU201_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

		}

	### Eurobonds ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU203_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU203_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Eurobonds"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU203_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU203_QMV_voted
							focus_EU203_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU203_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU203_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU203 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU203_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU203_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU203_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1203
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU203_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Eurobonds # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU203_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU203_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU203_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU203_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU203
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU203
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### Eurobonds retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU203_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU203_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU203 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU203_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU203
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU203_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU203_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU203_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU203_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU203_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU203
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU203_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU203_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU203_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU203
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU203_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU205_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU205
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU205_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Fiscal Union ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU206 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU206_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Fiscal Union"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU206
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU206_voted
							focus_EU206_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU206
			NOT = {
				focus_EU206_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU206 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU206_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU206_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU206_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1206
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU206_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Fiscal Union # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU206_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU206_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU206_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU206_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU206
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU206
					}
				}
		}
	}

						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}

		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU208_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU208_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU208
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU208
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### European Minister of Economy and Finance # Result Mission QMV ###

	### European Minister of Economy and Finance retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU208_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU208_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU208 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU208_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU208
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU208_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU208_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU208_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU208_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU208_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU208
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU208_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU208_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU208_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU208
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU208_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### EU Defense Policies ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU300 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU300_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus EU Defense Policies"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU300
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU300_voted
							focus_EU300_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU300
			NOT = {
				focus_EU300_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU300 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU300_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU300_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU300_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1300
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU300_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### EU Defense Policies ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU300_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU300_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

						NOT = {

							focus_EU300_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU300_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU300_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU300 }

			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU300_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU300_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1300
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU300_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Permanent Structured Cooperation (PESCO) ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU302_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU302_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Permanent Structured Cooperation (PESCO)"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU302_QMV_voted
							focus_EU302_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU302_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU302 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU302_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU302_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU302_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1302
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU302_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Permanent Structured Cooperation (PESCO) # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU302_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU302_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU302_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU302_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU302
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU302
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### Permanent Structured Cooperation (PESCO) # Result Mission QMV ###

	### Permanent Structured Cooperation (PESCO) retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU302_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU302_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU302 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU302_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU302
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU302_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU302_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU302_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU302
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU302_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU302
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU302_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU304
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU304_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### EuroArmy ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU305 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU305_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus EuroArmy"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU305
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU305_voted
							focus_EU305_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU305
			NOT = {
				focus_EU305_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU305 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU305_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU305_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU305_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1305
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU305_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU305_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU305_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU305_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU305_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU305
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU305
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### EU Permanent Member of the UNSC retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU307_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU307_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU307 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU307_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU307
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU307_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU307_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU307_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU307_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU307_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU307
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU307_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU307_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU307_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU307
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU307_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### EU Nuclear Power ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU308 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU308_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus EU Nuclear Power"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU308
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU308_voted
							focus_EU308_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU308
			NOT = {
				focus_EU308_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU308 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU308_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU308_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU308_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1308
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU308_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU401_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU401_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus General Data Protection Regulation"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU401_QMV_voted
							focus_EU401_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU401_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU401 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU401_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU401_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU401_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1401
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU401_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### General Data Protection Regulation # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU401_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU401_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU401_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU401_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU401
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU401
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### General Data Protection Regulation retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU401_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU401_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU401 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU401_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU401
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU401_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU401_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU401_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU401
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU401_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU401
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU401_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU403_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Relocation and Resettlement of Asylum Seekers ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU404 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU404_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Relocation and Resettlement of Asylum Seekers"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU404
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU404_voted
							focus_EU404_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU404
			NOT = {
				focus_EU404_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU404 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU404_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			NOT = {
					focus_EU405_accepted = yes
			}
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU404_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU404_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1404
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU404_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

					}
				}
		}

				clr_country_flag = focus_EU404_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU404_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU404
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU404_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU404
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU404_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

			}
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU406_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU406_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU406
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU406
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### European Asylum Agency retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU406_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU406_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU406 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU406_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU406
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU406_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU406_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU406_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU406
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU406_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU406
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU406_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Frontex ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU407 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU407_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Frontex"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU407
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU407_voted
							focus_EU407_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU407
			NOT = {
				focus_EU407_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU407 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU407_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU407_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU407_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1407
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU407_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Frontex ###

				value = 0
			}

					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }

		}
	}

	### European Commission Policies  ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU500_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU500_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus European Commission Policies "
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU500_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU500_QMV_voted
							focus_EU500_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU500_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU500_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU500 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU500_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU500_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU500_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1500
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU500_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### European Commission Policies  # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU500_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU500_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU500_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU500_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU500
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU500
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### European Commission Policies  retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU500_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU500_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU500 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU500_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU500
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU500_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU500_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU500_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU500_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU500_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU500
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU500_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU500_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU500_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU500
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU500_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU601
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU601_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### 2007 enlargement of the European Union ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU602 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU602_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus 2007 enlargement of the European Union"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU602
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU602_voted
							focus_EU602_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU602
			NOT = {
				focus_EU602_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU602 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU602_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU602_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU602_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1602
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU602_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1602
				}
			}

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}

	### 2007 enlargement of the European Union # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU602_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU602_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU602_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU602_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU602
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU602
					}
				}
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU602_retry

							#has_country_flag = focus_EU602
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU602_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU602
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU602
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU602_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU700_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU700_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU700
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU700
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### Withdrawal Policies # Result Mission QMV ###

	### Withdrawal Policies retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU700_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU700_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU700 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU700_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU700
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU700_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU700_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU700_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU700
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU700_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU700
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU700_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Article 50 ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU701 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU701_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Article 50"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU701
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU701_voted
							focus_EU701_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU701
			NOT = {
				focus_EU701_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU701 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU701_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU701_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU701_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1701
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU701_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Article 50 ###

				value = 0

				var = global.var_EUpopYes

				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}

				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1701
				}

	### No Deal Exit ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU703_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU703_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus No Deal Exit"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU703_QMV_voted
							focus_EU703_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU703_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU703 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU703_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			NOT = {
					focus_EU702_accepted = yes
			}
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU703_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU703_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1703
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU703_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### No Deal Exit # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU703_result = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU703_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU703_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU703_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU703
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU703
					}
				}
		}
	}
