	### No Deal Exit retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU703_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU703_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU703 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU703_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU703
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU703_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU703_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU703_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU703
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU703_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU703
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU703_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

				set_country_flag = focus_EU111_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU111
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU111_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### European Federation ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU112 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU112_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus European Federation"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU112
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU112_voted
							focus_EU112_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU112
			NOT = {
				focus_EU112_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU112 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU112_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			NOT = {
					focus_EU111_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = {
					focus_EU113_accepted = yes
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU112_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU112_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1112
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU112_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

		}

			has_global_flag = focus_EU604_voted

		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU604_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU604_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU604
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU604
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### Future enlargement of the European Union retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU604_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU604_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU604 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU604_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU604
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU604_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU604_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU604_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU604_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU604_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU604
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU604_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU604_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU604_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU604
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU604_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Western Balkans Enlargement ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU605 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU605_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Western Balkans Enlargement"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU605
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU605_voted
							focus_EU605_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU605
			NOT = {
				focus_EU605_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU605 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU605_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU605_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU605_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1605
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU605_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Western Balkans Enlargement ###

	### Black Sea Enlargement ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU607_QMV = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU607_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Black Sea Enlargement"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU607_QMV_voted
							focus_EU607_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV
			NOT = {
				focus_EU607_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU607 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU607_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU607_QMV_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU607_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1607
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU607_QMV_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}

	### Black Sea Enlargement # Result Decision ###

	EU_voting_mission_focus_EU607_result = {

		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			EU_voting_decision_result_trigger = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU607_voted
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		selectable_mission = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			focus_EU607_result = yes

		}
		timeout_effect = {
			focus_EU607_result = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU607
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						has_country_flag = focus_EU607
					}
				}
		}
	}

	### Black Sea Enlargement retry ###

	EU_voting_decision_EU607_retry = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU607_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU607 }
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = focus_EU607_retry
			has_idea = EU_member
				#NOT = {
					#any_country = {
						#OR = {
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU607
							#has_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV
						#}
					#}
				#}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU607_retry
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU607_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV_no
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU607_maj_no
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU607
				clr_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU607_EP_approval
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU607
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU607_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU609
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = european_constitution
						has_global_flag = european_federation
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU609_EP_overrule_option
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
					is_leader_of_EU_trade_policy = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = EU_no_retry
			}
		}
	}

	### Belarus ###

	EU_voting_decision_focus_EU610 = {
		#icon = EU_voting_decision

		available = {
			AND = {
				focus_EU610_EP_approval = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = "[ROOT.GetNameWithFlag] has completed National Focus Belarus"
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU610
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = focus_EU610_voted
							focus_EU610_accepted = yes
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = global.EU_member
								has_country_flag = EU_voted
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					influence_on_all_other_EU_members_3_percent = yes
					has_idea = EU_commission_president
					has_idea = EU_council_president
					has_idea = EU_parliament_president
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = focus_EU610
			NOT = {
				focus_EU610_accepted = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU610 }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = focus_EU610_retry }
			### voting mutually exclusive
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
			#
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = focus_EU610_voted
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteNo
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopNo
				value = 0
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
					NOT = { has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended }
				}
				EU_update_AI_focus_EU610_voting_modifier = yes
				country_event = {
					id = EUvote.1610
				}
			}
			activate_mission = EU_voting_mission_focus_EU610_result
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 210
		}
	}
